Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

On "Selling Writing for a Living" 250

— A Tan

In the second half of 1934, "The Writers' Group" launched an "attack" on "critics." Starting in 1934, Mr. Shen Congwen launched an attack on "Shanghai School" writers in the north (Tianjin), and Mr. Cao Juren gave him a strong answer, explaining that both the "Beijing School" and the "Shanghai School" should be swept away, and that between the two, it was better to be "Shanghai" than "Beijing."

In summary, the biggest accusation of Mr. Shen Congwen and others against the Shanghai School writers was "commercial competition." The so-called "commercial competition" here includes many things, but it reminds me of the matter of writers "selling writing for a living." "Selling writing for a living" translated into colloquial language is "writing to eat."

Originally, "writing to eat" is as proper as working to eat. Articles are essentially commodities. If they want to write something more meaningful and progressive, it's like a pharmacy selling cod liver oil and not selling arsenic. Of course, they may have other intentions besides making money, but this is just like a pharmacy owner who has the purpose of helping the world in addition to making money. Helping the world still doesn't prevent making money.

It is wrong for pharmacy owners to manufacture arsenic and aphrodisiacs just to make money. If the things that writers write are not feudal or erotic things written just to make money, then there is nothing wrong with them.

Almost every one of Dostoevsky's novels was forced out to repay debts or to make money to eat, but Dostoevsky is still the greatest realist writer in the world. So whether or not an article sells for money is irrelevant. What is important is whether the writer betrays his own ideas and the essence of art—truth—for money. What writers create through labor deserves wages or compensation.

But today, people are attacking people for "writing to eat," and those who are attacked are blushing and desperately trying to hide it. What is the reason for this?

In short, this is the relationship of awareness between the attacker and the attacked. Although they are standing in opposing positions, they have a common view that literature is noble and making money is vulgar. For a literary author to write articles and sell them for money is decadence. Any article written to make money is not a good article. Therefore, the attacker finds that the attacked writes articles to eat, as if they have discovered the other party's conspiracy and secrets, and raises it righteously. And the person being attacked seems to have really been discovered of a conspiracy and secrets, feeling anxious. The more you hide it, the more you feel that writing to eat is shameful, and the more advantageous it is for others to use this point to attack you. Of course, among those who hide their writing to eat, there must be those who betray their own ideas and the essence of art—truth—in order to make money, but these people are not within the scope of my discussion.

People who attack writing to eat generally have another profession. Let's not say that his reliance on that profession to eat is no different from writing to eat, but even the articles they write will never refuse royalties just because they have another profession. To put it bluntly, that article attacking others for writing to eat is written for royalties, or even for the sake of royalties.

We have long heard the famous saying "literature is useless." Now that articles can only be exchanged for food, it is already very miserable. (Of course, I am not saying that articles can secure the country and stabilize the people.) Moreover, with the storm of recession sweeping across, those who write to eat are about to "not even be full of the west wind." Adding to this the ridicule of those who don't write to eat, those who write to eat really only have one way out—to complain. If complaining is also writing to eat, then the only thing left to do is to starve to death. It is:

"Searching for chapters and picking sentences, old carving insects, the dawn moon hangs the jade bow against the curtain; not seeing the overflowing sea year after year, where does the article call the autumn wind?"

Seeing a Friend Off Southward 251

— Hui Ren

A sadness like mist wraps around my whole body.

With a lost heartscape, I tread with a dispirited pace from a corner of the city to see you off southward.

The river wind roars hoarsely over the waves, and blowing against my face and hands is so cold, like needles pricking my empty heart. That yellow steamboat, black smoke rings, and silver sky have been winking at me, and I have been gazing at them so greedily, wanting to carve them in my brain forever and ever, like a lover being separated.

The people are hysterical and noisy, as excited as soldiers going to the battlefield. I can only squeeze quietly into the crowd. Obviously, I don't have their joy, I am just so depressed, so sad.

I know I shouldn't show anything inauspicious when you're leaving. I've put on a mask and put on hypocrisy, calling out to you, but my hand is trembling so much, my heart is so bitter, I wish I could cry in your arms, but this expression of true emotion is said by some to be shameless and ridiculous; alas, how cruel society is!

But, you won't let sadness occupy your mindscape, you are happy and bright, like lovely spring light. These things, your eyes have told me. Of course, you should be happy, because you are about to fall back into the embrace of your hometown. At that time, your parents will smile at you, your brothers will greet you, and your little nephew will act coquettishly towards you. You will run into the valley to relive the fun after parting, and you will also breathe the fragrance of your hometown in the morning air, and you will also tell your family members about your feelings after separation.

Yes, you are happy, and I bless you, you will definitely blow the sea breeze of the East Sea carefree on the black night of your journey, and comfortably make sweet and fragrant dreams.

I will not be jealous of you, although I am somewhat reluctant for you to go south. Originally, I am not qualified to be your friend, I only have a lonely fate to live in a dark room and complain; I also only have a wandering fate, and soon I will leave this cursed city — Shanghai

I bless you, friend, may your journey be as bright as morning dew!

I bless you, girl, may your beauty be as beautiful as a rose, forever!

Night 252

— Zaimang

Night snatched away dusk, like a devil taking away a faint life; without resistance, without groaning, it, the dark night, occupied everything in space.

Look! This is the backstage of the drama stage of life.

Beauty may be ugliness, and hideous faces reveal more veins, all taking advantage of the night's cover to become active and dance! Night is mysterious to some!

"Come! Wine! Meat! Let's be wild! Let's get drunk! We have plenty of lust, and we also have plenty of money! Let's enjoy ourselves as much as possible! Before dawn replaces the night!"

However...

The multifaceted night revolves and revolves, grinding out overflowing wine foam, and at the same time grinding out the blood of life!

The clown put away his smile, only in the deep night does he caress his pain!

For the sake of life, they cut off pieces of their own flesh and sell them to people who are also "human beings"! That bloody smile!

During the day, excessive labor is not enough to keep them from being hungry, so at night, they have to sacrifice sleep! Work! Work! Is that result really for their own lives?

How many people whipped by society are twisting their brains in this long night!

Night! Why do you only give sweet dreams to some people, and trample the unfortunate even further under your feet? But, when the sun, like clear water, rises, where will you hide?

Is it Affectation? 253

— Maifu

Many foreigners do not know how to eat with Chinese chopsticks, and this is a fact. However, if you tell the villagers, they will not believe it. Many noble ladies and wives do not know how to use the rural outhouses. If you tell the people in the city, I'm afraid they won't believe it either. But this is also a fact.

Foreigners don't know how to use Chinese chopsticks because they haven't used them before, so that's why. Conversely, those ladies who don't know how to use rural outhouses are the same; they only use Western porcelain flush toilets, and when they see the simple wooden outhouses in the countryside, they will naturally panic.

Originally, things that have not been used, or things that have been abandoned for a long time, are difficult to use. For example, many high officials, having been away from their hometown for a long time, can't even speak the local dialect, which is the same principle. Because high officials also come from the countryside, but after all, they speak official language more often. In this way, people naturally evolve, and as a result, they readily abandon the unglamorous and unattractive local accent, which is only right and proper.

Although before there were porcelain toilets, ladies also had to use outhouses, but after all, that was the ladies of that time. This cannot be generalized. Every era has its own civilization, and every era has its own enjoyment. Therefore, when ordinary delicate ladies approach the dark and dirty outhouses in the countryside, they scream娇滴滴 (jiaodidi, a term for delicate and affected behavior) and are at a loss, which is probably right and proper.

Development of Contradictions 254

— Chen

Social scientists tell us that social phenomena are constantly in contradiction, and social evolution progresses step by step in contradiction. Therefore, contradiction is an element of evolution. Where there is contradiction, there is evolution. To seek evolution, one must also be based on contradiction. This has become a "law" of all changes in social affairs. China is scarred all over, riddled with wounds, and conflicts and contradictions are everywhere. Naturally, in this extreme "contradiction," applying this law will surely have extraordinary "development." Examining reality, there is indeed evidence to be found. However, China has "unique national conditions" and a unique environment, and its development and evolution must have its own "unusual" path.

Let's not talk about the future of the country and the fate of the nation, but only about the "unimportant" folk customs. Every time the electric lights are first lit and the neon lights shine, when we arrive at the central area of this Oriental Paris, we see that on both sides of the asphalt road, there are

迎風鹄立 (ying feng hu li, standing tall against the wind), lining up in formation, waiting for the opportunity to spread to people; and the towering hotels and many alleys and apartments also open the "doors of convenience" for those who buy a night of pleasure. Just counting within a day in Shanghai, in all of this, it is not known how many "germ" seeds are spread to many balcony guests. But if you take another glance at the street, there are countless hospitals and clinics with signs like "Specializing in gonorrhea and leucorrhea," "Guaranteed cure, never recurring," lined up one after another, fluttering in the wind. This phenomenon is naturally unavoidable "contradiction," but it can develop. The more "么二长三" (yao er chang san, a Shanghai dialect term for prostitutes), the more prosperous the venereal disease treatment business.

Furthermore, like "燕子窠" (yanzi ke, literally "swallow's nest," a term for opium dens), which are filled with addicted people day and night, its business is booming and its profits are a hundred times greater, which is far beyond what the "tightening" of the people's livelihoods can be compared to. However, when you penetrate this cloud-swallowing, fog-spitting atmosphere, there are small flyers and advertisements for "quitting smoking" and "blood purifying agents," and large, solemn prohibitions. This opposite fact must also be acknowledged as somewhat contradictory, but it can develop in contradiction. The stricter the ban, the further it is from a manifestation of the elimination of "雲土" (yuntu, slang for opium) and "人頭土" (rentoutu, more explicit slang for opium), and "寓禁於徵" (yu jin yu zheng, using prohibition to collect taxes) precisely illustrates the fact that under the "prohibition," general "elegant rooms" and "places for heart-to-heart talks" can greatly develop. On the surface, they are extremely conflicting, but in reality, they complement each other.

This kind of bizarre spectacle has become a special "unusual" way of contradictory development in Chinese social affairs. The so-called "development of contradiction" usually refers to the replacement of old conservative forces by new progressive forces in conflicts and defeats full of holes. However, the development of various social phenomena in China in contradiction is an increase in two opposing "contradictions." It is not "development of contradiction," but "developing contradictions."

Speaking of the root cause of China's poverty, as long as it is not concealed, everyone admits that it is endless infighting and civil war for years, and the reason why civil war occurs is that each side holds its own troops and guards its territory, claiming kingship. Therefore, China's large number of soldiers and courage in internal warfare are almost in an "contradictory" position with the phenomenon of national weakness, which cannot coexist. But because of the special "national conditions," the more impoverished it is, the more internal warfare and soldiers there are. The more wars and troops there are, the more impoverished China becomes. This "contradiction" has never been replaced by a new force and still becomes a "developing" phenomenon.

If you want to eliminate the phenomenon of "潇湘馆" (Xiaoxiang Pavilion, a residence in the novel Dream of the Red Chamber, often associated with elegance and sorrow) and "怡红院" (Yihong Courtyard, also from Dream of the Red Chamber, a place for entertainment with women) coexisting with hospitals for gonorrhea and leucorrhea, you must make a "ten-year-long Yangzhou dream" of repentance. To avoid the spectacle of hibiscus flowers everywhere and prohibitions all over the sky, you must also take a few "戒辟丸" (jiebi wan, pills for quitting bad habits). To save the morbid state of parallel development of poverty and war, if you feel that spiritual "sudden repentance" and internal "膏丹丸散" (gao dan wan san, medicinal pastes, pills, and powders) are ineffective, then I am afraid that there is only the method of surgery.

Amateur Mailbox

Bride Kidnapping 255

Editor:

I was introduced by friends and relatives to be engaged to a Mr. Wang, but we have not yet married. Now I hear that he does not intend to have a formal wedding, but wants to practice the vulgar custom of "bride kidnapping." Although my knowledge is shallow, I cannot help but feel resentful towards bride kidnapping. Therefore, I do not want to marry him. I want to publish a statement in the newspaper to dissolve the engagement and not be subject to this kind of restriction. However, I do not know if there are any regulations on this in the law. Therefore, I have written this letter to request a detailed answer. With respect, Li Shihao

Editor's note: "Bride kidnapping" is indeed an evil custom, and it is not recognized in law. You can dissolve the engagement because the other party wants to carry out bride kidnapping. Of course, we oppose this evil custom of "bride kidnapping"; however, this is only an illegal marriage procedure, and it is not that the other party is treating you badly. Therefore, we believe that you can temporarily not ask about the procedures for dissolving the engagement. You can now first think about whether you are willing to become a lifelong partner with the other party. If you are willing, then you should not dissolve the engagement. You can issue a warning to the other party, stating that you are determined not to accept "bride kidnapping" and not let him fantasize. But if the other party really cannot hold a grand wedding ceremony, then you should also forgive him and not be too demanding, and let him hold a simple wedding ceremony. If the other party can listen to this method, wouldn't it be much more satisfactory than "dissolving the engagement"? Of course, this method is based on the premise that "you are willing to marry him." If you do not love him and do not want to marry him, then it is best to dissolve the engagement.

"Dissolving the engagement" requires considerable legal procedures, and it cannot be done by publishing a statement in the newspaper. You should ask a lawyer about this issue.

Finally, we have a few words to say about "bride kidnapping."

The evil custom of "bride kidnapping" should also be eliminated, but we should also study the reasons for the occurrence of "bride kidnapping" and find ways to eliminate it. The main reason why "bride kidnapping" occurs is probably that the man's family is in economic difficulty and cannot hold a grand wedding ceremony. Of course, "marriage" is an extremely important and meaningful event in life. In theory, the "wedding ceremony" should be very elaborate, and relatives and friends should all be invited to have a lively celebration. However, for this reason, the level of expenses required for general "marriage" has been raised very high, so that among the people who disregard social disapproval, they practice "bride kidnapping" or other methods to avoid this difficulty. Those who love face borrow debts from all over the place and barely hold a wedding, which is a tragedy. People who marry by "bride kidnapping" will only often be ridiculed and mocked by others. People who marry by borrowing debts suffer unspeakable hardships. After marriage, they have to repay a large number of debts, and at the same time, the family's daily expenses are also greater than before. The number of people who feel economically panicked and oppressed throughout their lives because of marriage is countless. On the other hand, there are also things like late marriage and not marrying due to economic difficulties, but this is not a good solution either. Spending less money and incurring less debt on marriage is the right way. Therefore, we now very much advocate the "simplification" and "economization" of wedding ceremonies, hoping that in the future, we will no longer "bury the pain of a lifetime of enduring阴霾 (yinmai, haze, gloom)" in a joyous ceremony filled with guests and joy.

Lonely People (4) 256

— Daini

Kejia suddenly raised his head, rubbing his eyelids, not believing that he had seen the wrong person, and asked in surprise, "Eh! You..."

"Sleeping so soundly, where were you last night?" the woman asked sarcastically.

"Don't tease, it's all because of little brother," Kejia pointed to Xiaoxun and explained, then asked, "Did you just arrive in Shanghai today too?"

"It's my sister's wedding." Before he could finish speaking, he smiled beautifully at Xiaoxun. Although Xiaoxun was meeting her for the first time, he knew that she was Jingyi's older sister, Jingwen. Naturally, Jingwen was also familiar with the name Zhu Xiaoxun. However, "little brother," that strange and inappropriate title, she did not expect that it would be this brother-in-law's old friend. Xiaoxun understood what she meant and acted shy. "Ha." Without losing his wild bull nature, he punched himself,

"Introduced his sister's 'sister,' Hu Jingwen."

After a crude introduction, he began his speech:

"At the end of last year, I forced little brother to come to Hangzhou to recuperate, at least half of it was his own volition. I am often unable to deal with this wild horse that has broken free of its reins. Recently, he wrote a letter that was like a complaint, so I specially came to Hangzhou to invite him to Shanghai. Jingwen, do you know what he said?" He paused, seemingly waiting for the two to answer. "He wanted to come to Shanghai after my wedding, because he | couldn't bear to see a woman. Haha."

"Mr. Zhu, is that true?" Naturally, the teasing story made Jingwen suspicious. Xiaoxun smiled helplessly, shaking his naturally curly hair. "Is it not true?" He straightened his back, looking like a real athlete. "Then, who is that woman?" "It's your classmate, Xu Qinbo." "What's so unbearable about seeing her?" "Ask little brother." Xiaoxun nervously glared at Kejia. If possible, he would immediately return to Hangzhou. In front of a woman, he could neither show off his skin, nor was he afraid that the innocent Jingwen would ask, "Mr. Zhu, what exactly is going on?" He admittedly failed to pick out a book from his briefcase, avoiding the other person's gaze.

As for Kejia, although he was honest and unceremonious, he also knew that in this situation, he could not make Zhu Xiaoxun the focus of the conversation. He coughed a few times to clear his throat and changed the subject.

"Jingwen, did you receive her letter?" "The letter was received early..." A clever woman, she understood everything, her attitude became very serious. "The school didn't have a suitable substitute teacher for a while, and finally the principal took over temporarily, so I was finally able to get away today. I want to find a job in Shanghai next semester. My sister is married, so I can't marry my mom too..."

Xiaoxun laughed as he listened. He casually closed the novel that he had been flipping through on the first page. Kejia seized the opportunity to take out a cigarette, which finally broke the gloomy situation.

The three people smoked cigarettes, scattering them into the March spring breeze, gently.

The car body shook leisurely, a sharp whistle sounded, and slowly drove into Fengjing Station. Kejia raised his fat palm and reached out the window to grab a vendor. Xiaoxun, as if he had gotten an opportunity, leaned behind Kejia and said, "My sister likes to eat Fengjing pig trotters, buy a few baskets to take with you."

The wild bull had already picked up four baskets, he didn't taste Xiaoxun's words carefully, another teasing!

"Little brother, when did your mom give birth to little sister?"

"My sister's 'sister' Hu Jingyi." He smiled victoriously, shaking his naturally curly hair. "In that case, my mom didn't | didn't get married together with my sister." Nervous laughter, innocent laughter, unnatural smiles, burying all sorrow behind joy.
